***келья.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:келья.html>ке́лья</a> (14166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">келиꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kelija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κελλία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kellía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, plural of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κελλίον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kellíon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">garret</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κέλλα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kélla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cella</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:келья.html>ке́лья</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kélʹja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:келья.html>ке́льи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:келья.html>ке́льи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:келья.html>ке́лий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cell <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">room in a monastery for sleeping one person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">camping</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кемпинг.html>ке́мпинг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kɛ́mpinɡ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кемпинг.html>ке́мпинга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кемпинг.html>ке́мпинги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кемпинг.html>ке́мпингов</a></b>)|or|ке́мпинг//kémping|}}
</p>
<ol><li>camping ground, campground, campsite, camp</li>
<li>camping</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ке́м<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пинг</b>
</p><p>Существительное, неодушевлённое, мужской род, 2-е склонение (тип склонения 3a  по классификации А. А. Зализняка).
</p><p>Корень: <b>-кемпинг-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение">Значение</span></h4>
<ol><li>лагерь для автотуристов с оборудованной парковкой, туалетами, местами для палаток или домиками лёгкого типа <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">Прокладка маршрутов, строительство <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">кемпингов</span>, дорог и мотелей, все экономические расчёты строятся на том, что 90 процентов путешествий в Америке совершается в автомобиле. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i>Василий Песков, Борис Стрельников, «Земля за океаном», <span class="example-date">1977</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кесарев.html>ке́сарев</a> (27727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">késarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ев</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ev</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарев.html>ке́сарев</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">késarev</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Caesarean, Caesar's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарев.html>ке́сарево</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сечение.html>сече́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>késarevo</b> sečénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Caesarean</b> section</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарев.html>ке́сарево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">késarju <b>késarevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">render unto Caesar</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">unto Caesar [the things that are] <b>Caesar’s</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***кесарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарь</a> (23416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kesarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Koine_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Koine Greek">Koine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Καῖσαρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kaîsar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Caesar</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">це́зарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cézarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><span class="serial-comma">,</span><span class="serial-and"> and</span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">це́сарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">césarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">késarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́саря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сари</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Caesar <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">title of a Roman or Byzantine emperor</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кесарь.html>ке́сарю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кесарев.html>ке́сарево</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>késarju</b> késarevo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">render unto <b>Caesar</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">unto Caesar [the things that are] Caesar’s</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***кефир.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́р</a> (10447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed into Russian from a language of the Caucausus; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mingrelian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mingrelian language">Mingrelian</a></span> <i class="Geor mention" lang="xmf">ქიფური</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xmf-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kipuri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ossetian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ossetian language">Ossetian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="os">къӕпы</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="os-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k’æpy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karachay-Balkar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Karachay-Balkar language">Karachay-Balkar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="krc">гыпы</i>. The ultimate origin is unknown.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kefír</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>kefir (a yogurt-like beverage made from fermented cows' milk)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обожать.html>обожа́ю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́р</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зато.html>зато́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja prósto obožáju <b>kefír</b>, no zató terpétʹ ne mogú molokó!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I just love kefir, but, on the other hand, I hate milk!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ке<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>фи́р</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кефир-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***кибитка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кибитка.html>киби́тка</a> (27155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested since the middle of the 17th century. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кибита́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kibitá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arched hoop, half of a hoop of a large fish-trap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, obsolete (17th c.) <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">киби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kibítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arc of the bow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:кибитка.html>киби́тка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kybýtka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">кібі́тка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kibítka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>: compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">кибет</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kibet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">кибет</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kibet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kipchak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kipchak language">Kipchak</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="qwm-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kebit</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="qwm-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kibit</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="qwm-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kabit</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stall, shop</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karakhanid_language" class="extiw" title="w:Karakhanid language">Karakhanid</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xqa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">käbit</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Probably ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sogdian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Sogdian language">Sogdian</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sog-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qpyδ</span> <span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/kəpēδ/</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">کلبه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolbe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see it for more), though <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">قُبَّة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qubba</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dome</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> too is often mentioned as another possible ultimate source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кибитка.html>киби́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kibítka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кибитка.html>киби́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кибитка.html>киби́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кибитка.html>киби́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>kibitka <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">horse-drawn carriage</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>yurt, kibitka <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">nomad's dwelling of some ethnic groups such as the Kalmyks and Kyrgyz</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>telega or sleigh with a (usually rounded) cover over the passenger seats</li></ol>

***кивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кивать.html>кива́ть</a> (2839)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кивать.html>кива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кивнуть.html>кивну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to nod, to beckon</li>
<li>to motion, to point, to allude</li></ol>

<p><b>ки<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:кивнуть.html>кивну́ть</a>.

***кидать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кидать.html>кида́ть</a> (5007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kydati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кидать.html>кида́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kidátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to fling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to abandon, to leave behind <i>(somebody)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cheat, to swindle</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кидать.html>кида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кидаться.html>кида́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kidátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуться.html>ки́нуться</a></b>)

<li>to dash, to rush</li>

<p><b>ки<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
